<t>CREATE TABLE Hotel (
    hotel_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    location VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    rating FLOAT
);

CREATE TABLE Room (
    room_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    hotel_id INT REFERENCES Hotel(hotel_id),
    room_type VARCHAR(50),
    price DECIMAL(10, 2),
    capacity INT
);

CREATE TABLE Booking (
    booking_id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    room_id INT REFERENCES Room(room_id),
    guest_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    check_in_date DATE,
    check_out_date DATE,
    total_price DECIMAL(10, 2)
);</t><s>UPSERT INTO Hotel (hotel_id, name, location, rating) VALUES (1, 'Hotel ABC', 'New York', 4.5) ON CONFLICT (hotel_id) DO UPDATE SET name = EXCLUDED.name, location = EXCLUDED.location, rating = EXCLUDED.rating;</s>
